`timescale 1ns/1ps

module surfboard #(
	parameter int W = 24,
	parameter bit SIGNED = 1
)(
	input  logic [W-1:0] A [0:799],
	input  logic [W-1:0] B [0:799],
	output logic [SUMW-1:0] C [0:799]
);
	localparam int PROD_W = 2*W;
	localparam int SUMW   = PROD_W + 1;

	logic signed   [W-1:0] As [0:799];
	logic signed   [W-1:0] Bs [0:799];
	logic          [W-1:0] Au [0:799];
	logic          [W-1:0] Bu [0:799];

	assign Au = A; assign Bu = B;
	assign As = A; assign Bs = B;

	function automatic logic [W-1:0] mul(input int i, input int j);
		logic [PROD_W-1:0] tempResult;
		if (SIGNED)
			tempResult = As[i] * Bs[j];
		else
			tempResult = Au[i] * Bu[j];
		mul = tempResult[3*(2*PROD_W)/4 - 2: PROD_W/4 - 1];
	endfunction

	assign C[0] = mul(0,0) + mul(1,40) + mul(2,80) + mul(3,120) + mul(4,160) + mul(5,200) + mul(6,240) + mul(7,280) + mul(8,320) + mul(9,360) + mul(10,400) + mul(11,440) + mul(12,480) + mul(13,520) + mul(14,560) + mul(15,600) + mul(16,640) + mul(17,680) + mul(18,720) + mul(19,760) + mul(20,800) + mul(21,840) + mul(22,880) + mul(23,920) + mul(24,960) + mul(25,1000) + mul(26,1040) + mul(27,1080) + mul(28,1120) + mul(29,1160);
